导出zpool：                zpool export stripedpool
                           # zpool create dozer mirror /file/a /file/b
导出zpool：                # zpool export dozer
查看有哪些zpool可以import：# zpool import -d /file
查看有哪些zpool可以import：  zpool import
zpool import stripedpool

                    zpool create geekpool  c1t1d0
Using files:        mkfile 100m file1
                    zpool create geekpool /file1
Using disk slices   zpool create geekpool c1t1d0s0
Dynamic strip:      zpool create geekpool c1t1d0   c1t2d0
                    once a disk is added in this fashion to a zfs pool may not be removed from the pool again. Only way to free the disk is to destroy entire pool. This happens due to the dynamic striping nature of the pool which uses both disk to store the data.
                    
Mirrored pool:      zpool create geekpool mirror   c1t1d0 c1t2d0
                    zpool create geekpool mirror   c1t1d0 c1t2d0 c1t3d0
                    zpool attach zeepool        c1t1d0 c2t1d0       #Converting a Two-Way Mirrored Storage Pool to a Three-way Mirrored Storage Pool
					zpool add    mpool   mirror c6t0d0p0 c7t0d0p0   #Enlarging a mirrored pool, add two more disks to enhance the file system

					
					zpool create geekpool raidz  c1t1d0 c1t2d0 c1t3d0
					zpool create geekpool raidz2 c1t1d0 c1t2d0 c1t3d0
					zpool create geekpool raidz3 c1t1d0 c1t2d0 c1t3d0 c1t4d0
添加strip的硬盘：
          zpool add zones  c1t2d0
					dry run :  zpool  add -n  zones  c1t2d0

Adding spare device to zpool:
                    zpool add geekpool spare c1t3d0
                    zpool autoreplace=on mpool
					
Creating a ZFS Storage Pool With Cache Devices:					
                    zpool create tank mirror c2t0d0 c2t1d0 c2t3d0 cache c2t5d0 c2t8d0
					
Dry run on zpool creation:
					zpool create -n geekpool raidz2 c1t1d0 c1t2d0 c1t3d0

``````````zpool disk```````````
zpool clear tank
zpool clear tank c1t0d0
zpool replace tank c1t1d0
zpool replace tank c1t1d0 c1t2d0  #replacing a device in a storage pool with a disk in a different physical location, you will need to specify both devices.		

zpool scrub  tank
zpool scrub -s tank  #You can stop a scrubbing operation that is in progress by using the -s option
zpool status tank    #To view the resilvering process
zpool status -v tank #display a list of file names with persistent errors

1.Offline the disk, if necessary, with the zpool offline command.
2.Remove the disk to be replaced.
3.Insert the replacement disk.
4.Run the zpool replace command. For example:
  zpool replace tank c1t1d0
  zpool replace zones c0t5000C50098985CA3d0  c0t5000CCA249D133C3d0
                      旧盘                   新盘
                      根据man手册，同槽位替换硬盘必须指定新盘

6.Bring the disk online with the zpool online command.


Repairing ZFS Storage Pool-Wide Damage
zpool status
zpool clear -F tpool
zpool import -o readonly=on tpool
zpool destroy -f

把snapshot从一台机器移动到另一台机器
zfs send -R zones/$UUID-disk0@last-snapshot | ssh destination-host zfs receive zones/$UUID-disk0
#Then you need to send the VM's metadata and create the VM. The JSON command updates the metadata so that vmadm doesn't attempt to create the ZFS datasets.
vmadm get $UUID | json -e "for(i in this.disks){this.disks[i].nocreate=true;}this.i=undefined;" | ssh destination-host vmadm create

tee /opt/dsapid.json <<-'EOF'
    { 
      "brand": "joyent", 
      "image_uuid": "a0e719d6-4e21-11e4-92eb-2bf6399552e7", 
      "autoboot": true, 
      "alias": "dsapid-server",
      "hostname": "datasets.dsapid", 
      "resolvers": [ "114.114.114.114", "8.8.4.4" ], 
      "max_physical_memory": 1024, 
      "max_swap": 1024,
      "tmpfs": 1024, 
      "quota": 120, 
      "nics": [ { "nic_tag": "admin", "ip": "10.0.1.160", "netmask": "255.255.255.0", "gateway": "10.0.1.1","primary": true } ],
      "internal_metadata": {
              "root_pw": "root",
              "admin_pw": "admin"
              },
      "customer_metadata": {
                 "user-script" : "/usr/bin/sed -i.bak 's/PermitRootLogin without-password/PermitRootLogin yes/g'   /etc/ssh/sshd_config; /usr/bin/sed -i.bak2 's/PasswordAuthentication no/PasswordAuthentication yes/g'   /etc/ssh/sshd_config; /usr/sbin/svcadm restart svc:/network/ssh:default"

              }
    }
EOF
vmadm create -f /opt/dsapid.json

 echo "root:root" |changepass

```````在global zone安装salt```````````
相关讨论：                   https://github.com/saltstack/salt/issues/31446
自己编译global zone包的步骤：https://github.com/saltstack/salt/blob/develop/pkg/smartos/esky/BUILD_ENVIRONMENT.md
在global zone安装方法：
步骤0：安装pkgin
cd /
curl -k http://192.168.1.128/smartos/bootstrap-2016Q3-x86_64.tar.gz | gzcat | tar -xf -
#或curl -k http://pkgsrc.joyent.com/packages/SmartOS/bootstrap/bootstrap-2015Q2-x86_64.tar.gz | gzcat | tar -xf -
pkg_admin rebuild
#pkgin -y up
pkgin install zeromq #最新版要独立安装zeromq
步骤1：从 http://pkg.blackdot.be/extras/ 上下载salt-2016.3.3-esky-smartos.tar.gz 
或：
cd /opt/
wget http://192.168.1.128/file-share/salt-2016.3.3-esky-smartos.tar.gz   
echo 10.75.1.70 salt>>/etc/hosts&&cd /opt && tar   zxvf   salt-2016.3.3-esky-smartos.tar.gz && /opt/salt/install/install.sh && svcadm enable salt-minion
svcadm restart salt-minion

用ansible安装salt等：
 ansible hp  -f 1 -m raw -a "echo 10.0.1.38 salt>>/etc/hosts;cd /;curl -k httts;cd /;curl -k http://salt/smartos/bootstrap-2016Q3-x86_64.tar.gz | gzcat |/ tar -xf -;pkg_admin rebuild;cd /opt/;wget http://salt/file-share/salt-2016.3.3-esky-smartos.tar.gz   ;cd /opt ; tar   zxvf   salt-2016.3.3-esky-smartos.tar.gz ;/opt/salt/install/install.sh && svcadm enable salt-minion;svcadm restart salt-minion"
ansible hp  -f 1 -m raw -a "imgadm sources -a  http://images.briphant.com; imgadm sources -d  https://images.joyent.com"
ansible hp  -f 1 -m raw -a "imgadm import 1bd84670-055a-11e5-aaa2-0346bb21d5a1"
````global zone 重启``````
global zone 重启后/etc/hosts内容和id_rsa消失，做如下操作来恢复：：
echo 10.75.1.70 salt>>/etc/hosts;svcadm restart salt-minion;ssh-keygen -f $HOME/.ssh/id_rsa -t rsa -N ''
#注：10.75.1.70是salt master的地址，salt默认把hostname当作minion id的名字

=========smartos ssh section================

svcadm restart svc:/network/ssh:default

=======smartos memory section =========
echo ::memstat | mdb -k

prtconf | grep Memory

============ ipv6 section =============

To disable ip v6 in the running system:
echo 1 > /proc/sys/net/ipv6/conf/all/disable_ipv6
echo 1 > /proc/sys/net/ipv6/conf/default/disable_ipv6

centos:
  diable ipv6:
sysctl -w net.ipv6.conf.all.disable_ipv6=1
sysctl -w net.ipv6.conf.default.disable_ipv6=1

  enable ipv6
sysctl -w net.ipv6.conf.all.disable_ipv6=0
sysctl -w net.ipv6.conf.default.disable_ipv6=0

debian:


============smartos disk===========================
format < /dev/null | sed -n 's/.*\(<.*>\).*/\1/p' 
zpool replace zones c0t5000C5006349E003d0 <new disk>
获取硬盘槽位号
步骤1
zpool status

c0t5000C500626E601Bd0  FAULTED      1   628     0  too many errors
5000c500626e601b  is the target ID of the physical disk.
································
        NAME                       STATE     READ WRITE CKSUM
        zones                      DEGRADED     0     0     0
          mirror-0                 ONLINE       0     0     0
            c0t5000C500626DD6A7d0  ONLINE       0     0     0
            c0t5000C500626DA9FFd0  ONLINE       0     0     0
          mirror-1                 DEGRADED     0     0     0
            c0t5000C500626E601Bd0  FAULTED      1   628     0  too many errors
            c0t5000C500626DE48Fd0  ONLINE       0     0     0
        logs
          c0t55CD2E404B735D0Cd0    ONLINE       0     0     0
··························
步骤2
prtconf -v   搜索关键字 name='wwn' 和 5000c500626e601b
                mpt_sas#2 (online)
                        name='wwn' type=string items=1
                            value='5000c500626e601b'
                        name='lun' type=int items=1
                            value=00000000
                        name='lun64' type=int64 items=1
                            value=0000000000000000
                        name='target-port' type=string items=1
                            value='w5000c500626e6019'
                        name='attached-port' type=string items=1
                            value='w500605b001bdd518'
                        name='obp-path' type=string items=1
                            value='/pci@0,0/pci8086,e04@2/pci1000,3020@0/disk@w5000c500626e6019,0'
                        name='phy-num' type=int items=1
                            value=00000001
                        name='path-class' type=string items=1
                            value='primary'
phy-num 槽位号是1号

``````````smartos pxe section`````````````

1、dnsmasq根据 /opt/local/etc/dnsmasq.conf配置，获得ip地址
2、dnsmasq根据 dhcp-boot=pxegrub配置项，/tftpboot中下载pxegrub程序
3、pxegrub程序 从boot/grub/menu.lst启动smartos，boot/grub/menu.lst位于/tftpboot中
4、boot目录是从smartos-20160721T174418Z.iso解压出来的，smartos-20160721T174418Z.iso出来的内容放在/tftpboot中


#先创建虚拟机
            tee /opt/smartos_vm.json <<-'EOF'            
            {
             "brand": "joyent",
             "image_uuid": "1bd84670-055a-11e5-aaa2-0346bb21d5a1",
             "alias": "pxe",
             "hostname": "pxe",
             "max_physical_memory": 1024,
             "quota": 50,
             "resolvers": ["10.0.1.1", "114.114.114.114"],
             "nics": [
                {
                        "nic_tag": "admin",
                        "ip": "10.0.1.250",
                        "netmask": "255.255.255.0",
                        "dhcp_server": "1",
                        "primary": true
                }
             ],
             "internal_metadata": {
              "root_pw": "root",
              "admin_pw": "admin"
              },
             "customer_metadata": {
                 "user-script" : "/usr/bin/sed -i.bak 's/PermitRootLogin without-password/PermitRootLogin yes/g'   /etc/ssh/sshd_config; /usr/sbin/svcadm restart svc:/network/ssh:default"

              }
            }			
EOF

`````pxegrub section ```
#tftp

pkgin -fy up
pkgin -y install tftp-hpa
mkdir /tftpboot
echo "tftp dgram udp wait root /opt/local/sbin/in.tftpd in.tftpd -s /tftpboot" > /tmp/tftp.inetd
svcadm enable inetd
inetconv -i /tmp/tftp.inetd -o /tmp
svccfg import /tmp/tftp-udp.xml
svcadm restart tftp/udp

`````smartos dnsmasq section``````
pkgin -y install dnsmasq
mv /opt/local/etc/dnsmasq.conf /opt/local/etc/dnsmasq.conf.bak
tee /opt/local/etc/dnsmasq.conf <<-'EOF'
   #Lease File to track leases
   dhcp-leasefile=/etc/dnsmasq.leases
   # Give out addresses in the 172.16.0.1/24 subnet
   dhcp-range=10.0.1.210,10.0.1.215,255.255.255.0,2h
   # The name of the boot file is pxegrub
   dhcp-boot=pxegrub
EOF
svcadm enable dnsmasq



pkgin -y install wget

wget  -O  /tftpboot/pxegrub    http://salt/file-share/pxelinux/pxegrub
#或wget  -O  /tftpboot/pxegrub     http://aszeszo.googlepages.com/pxegrub
   #在centos上 执行
   #wget  -O  /root/latest.iso http://192.168.1.128/file-share/smartos-20160721T174418Z.iso
   #mount -o loop  /root/latest.iso    /root/mnt/

scp -r  xx.xx.xx.xx:/root/mnt/*    /tftpboot/
＃说明：xx.xx.xx.xx是centos的ip 地址
#问题定位，关闭dnsmaq服务，用dnsmasq调试模式：svcadm disable dnsmasq ;/opt/local/sbin/dnsmasq -C /opt/local/etc/dnsmasq.conf -d

````````pxelinux section``````
方法一：在centos上
yum -y install syslinux
mkdir -p /var/lib/tftpboot/pxelinux/pxelinux.cfg
mkdir -p /var/lib/tftpboot/pxelinux/smartos/

sudo tee /etc/dnsmasq.d/smartos.conf<<-'EOF'
interface=enp0s8
dhcp-range=10.0.1.190,10.0.1.200,6h
#dhcp-host=80:00:27:c6:a1:16,10.0.0.253,svr1,infinite
dhcp-boot=pxelinux/pxelinux.0
enable-tftp
tftp-root=/var/lib/tftpboot
EOF

cp /usr/share/syslinux/pxelinux.0 /var/lib/tftpboot/pxelinux/pxelinux.0

wget -O  /var/lib/tftpboot/pxelinux/smartos/ldlinux.c32   http://salt/file-share/pxelinux/ldlinux.c32
wget -O  /var/lib/tftpboot/pxelinux/smartos/libcom32.c32  http://salt/file-share/pxelinux/libcom32.c32
wget -O  /var/lib/tftpboot/pxelinux/smartos/mboot.c32     http://salt/file-share/pxelinux/mboot.c32

scp -r ./platform/   10.0.1.101:/var/lib/tftpboot/pxelinux/
tee  /var/lib/tftpboot/pxelinux/pxelinux.cfg/default<<-'EOF'
EOF


说明：/var/lib/tftpboot/pxelinux/pxelinux.cfg/default 配置文件中需要的mboot.c32文件，此文件版本pxelinux.0的版本必须一致，都是从syslinux-4.05.tar.gz中取出。
[root@NAT_Server ~]# sudo yum list installed| grep syslinux
                    syslinux.x86_64                      4.05-13.el7                    @base       
[root@NAT_Server ~]# wget https://www.kernel.org/pub/linux/utils/boot/syslinux/syslinux-4.05.tar.gz
[root@NAT_Server ~]# cp ./syslinux-4.05/com32/mboot/mboot.c32    /var/lib/tftpboot/pxelinux/smartos/
[root@NAT_Server ~]# cp /usr/share/syslinux/pxelinux.0 /var/lib/tftpboot/pxelinux/pxelinux.0

·············
方法二：在smartos上
mkdir -p /tftpboot/pxelinux.cfg
cp ./syslinux-4.05/core/pxelinux.0 /tftpboot/

tee  /tftpboot/pxelinux.cfg/default<<-'EOF'

EOF
#/usr/xpg4/bin/find  ./ -path  "*mboot.c32"
#/usr/xpg4/bin/find  ./ -path  "*ldlinux.c32"
#/usr/xpg4/bin/find  ./ -path  "*libcom32.c32"

#/tftpboot/ 目录是pxe获取文件的默认路径
find  -E   ./   -iregex  ".*(ldlinux.c32|bios.*Mboot.c32|bios.*libcom32.c32|/pxelinux.0)"|xargs -I{} cp {} /tftpboot/  
smaortos: find    ./  -regextype posix-extended   -iregex  ".*(ldlinux.c32|bios.*Mboot.c32|bios.*libcom32.c32|/pxelinux.0)"

#/tftpboot/pxelinux.cfg/default文件中配置使用/tftpboot/smartos下的mboot.c32
cp /root/syslinux-6.03/bios/com32/mboot/mboot.c32 /tftpboot/smartos    

sudo tee /opt/local/etc/dnsmasq.conf<<-'EOF'
#Lease File to track leases
dhcp-leasefile=/etc/dnsmasq.leases
# Give out addresses in the 172.16.0.1/24 subnet
dhcp-range=10.0.1.210,10.0.1.215,255.255.255.0,2h
# The name of the boot file is pxelinux.0
dhcp-boot=pxelinux.0
EOF

方法三：
在centos上获取pxelinux相关文件：
  步骤一：
  wget https://www.kernel.org/pub/linux/utils/boot/syslinux/syslinux-6.03.tar.gz
  find    ./   -regextype posix-extended  -iregex  ".*(ldlinux.c32|bios.*Mboot.c32|bios.*libcom32.c32|/pxelinux.0)"
  步骤二：
  把找出来的文件拷贝到smartos上
````````ipxe section````````
svcadm restart  dnsmasq
简单方案:
wget -O  /tftpboot/undionly.kpxe   http://cuddletech.com/IPXE-100612_undionly.kpxe
或 wget -O  /tftpboot/undionly.kpxe   http://boot.ipxe.org/undionly.kpxe
或 wget -O  /tftpboot/smartos/platform-latest.tgz http://salt/iso/platform-20170216T015949Z.tgz
tar zxvf  ./platform-latest.tgz 
tee smartos.ipxe <<-'EOF' 
#!ipxe
# /var/lib/tftpboot/smartos.ipxe.tpl
kernel /smartos/platform-20170216T015949Z/i86pc/kernel/amd64/unix -B smartos=true
initrd /smartos/platform-20170216T015949Z/i86pc/amd64/boot_archive
boot
EOF

=========smartos rsyslog=============
rsyslogd -v 3检查rsyslog版本号
global zone使用 rsyslog 5.8 版本的日志服务:

   /etc/rsyslog.conf
   svcadm refresh svc:/system/system-log
   svcs           svc:/system/system-log:default


native zone使用 rsyslog 7  版本的日志服务:

   /opt/local/etc/rsyslog.conf
   svcadm disable svc:/pkgsrc/rsyslog:default

====screen section====
sudo yum -y install screen
1. type screen command
2. typing “CTRL + A”, followed by “?”
   #By typing “CTRL + A” you state that the next signal is to be sent to the program “screen“, 
   in stead of to the Shell (like you would in a normal shell). You’ll see a list of all bindings known to “screen“.
   
``````   
screen -ls
    List all screen terminals :the list will contain the following information :


	* the state of the screen terminals ( Attached , Detached)
	* the PID of of each screen terminal
	* the name of each screen terminal
	
screen  -r  nnnn
      Enable a session with screen terminal that has PID  “nnnn”  (see screen -ls)

========jobs section===========
    如何使得命令进入后台
	方法一： Appending an ampersand ( & ) to the command runs the job in the background.
	  find / -ctime -1 > /tmp/changed-file-list.txt &
	方法二： 
	  步骤1： Press ‘CTRL+Z’ which will suspend the current foreground job.
	  步骤2： Execute bg to make that command to execute in background.
	  举例：
	  # find / -ctime -1 > /tmp/changed-file-list.txt 
	  # [CTRL-Z] [2]+ Stopped find / -ctime -1 > /tmp/changed-file-list.txt 
	  # bg
	管理后台正在执行的命令：
	
	1. jobs命令
	   举例：
	   [1] Running bash download-file.sh & 
	   [2]- Running evolution & 
	   [3]+ Done nautilus .
	2. fg command. When executed without arguments, it will take the most recent background job to the foreground.
	   # fg %1
	   # kill %2

=========smartos timezone section=========
pkgin -y install smtools;sm-set-timezone Asia/Shanghai
salt 'jinhao'  cmd.run 'pkgin -y install smtools;sm-set-timezone Asia/Shanghai'  shell='/usr/bin/bash' -t 1200   #注意shell参数要带单引号
rtc -z Asia/Shanghai
salt home_fifo cmd.run "rtc -z Asia/Shanghai"
salt home_fifo cmd.run "rtc -c"

````````````````
native zone修改时区，经验值有效
salt home_fifo timezone.get_zone
salt home_fifo cmd.run "sed -i.bak2 's/TZ=UTC/TZ=Asia\/Shanghai/' /etc/TIMEZONE"
salt home_fifo cmd.run "diff /etc/TIMEZONE /etc/TIMEZONE.bak2"
salt home_fifo cmd.run "reboot"

========string section==========chenge file name=========

${string/pattern/replacement}
ls *.new |xargs -I {} sh -c 'a={};b=${a/new/0.7};mv {}  $b'  #把.new文件改成.0.7文件


==========json section ==========


Use the -e CODE option to execute code on the input JSON.

           $ echo ´{"name":"trent","age":38}´ | json -e ´age++´
           {
             "name": "trent",
             "age": 39
           }

Set a key to undefined to remove it
           $ echo ´{"one": 1, "two": 2}´ | json -e ´this.one=undefined´
           {"two":2}

看 man json 获得更多帮助
`````````````json section`````````node.js section````````````````
在linux中使用json命令：

docker 命令行方式：
docker pull node
docker run -i --rm --name json  -v "$PWD":/usr/src/app -w /usr/src/app node:latest node --version
curl -L https://github.com/trentm/json/raw/master/lib/json.js > json.js
echo '{"one": 1, "two": 2}'  | docker run -i --rm --name json  -v "$PWD":/usr/src/app -w /usr/src/app node:latest node json.js  -e 'this.one=undefined'
echo '{"name":"trent","age":38}'   | docker run -i --rm --name json  -v "$PWD":/usr/src/app -w /usr/src/app node:latest node json.js    -e 'this.age++

````
docker bash方式：
docker run -it --rm --name json  -v "$PWD":/usr/src/app -w /usr/src/app node:latest /bin/bash
npm install -g json
json --version
